### [227] [Holistic Evaluation and Failure Diagnosis of AI Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14865)
*Netta Madvil,Gilad Dym,Alon Mecilati,Edo Dekel,Jonatan Liberman,Rotem Brazilay,Liron Schliesser,Max Svidlo,Shai Nir,Orel Shalom,Yaron Friedman,David Connack,Amos Rimon,Philip Tannor,Shir Chorev*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结合 agent 级诊断与 span 级评估的 AI Agent 评估框架，能在长执行轨迹中更准确地定位并分类错误，在 TRAIL/GAIA/SWE-Bench 上显著优于现有方法，说明评估方法比模型能力更关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 AI Agent 评估方法存在两类核心不足：结果级指标只能给出成功或失败，无法解释原因；过程级方法难以把具体失败类型精确定位到长而结构化的执行轨迹中的位置。

Method: 论文提出一种整体式 Agent 评估框架，将自顶向下的 agent 级诊断与自底向上的 span 级评估结合起来，把长轨迹分析分解为相互独立的逐 span 判断，并为每个判断生成 span 级理由。

Result: 在 TRAIL 基准上，该框架在 GAIA 和 SWE-Bench 的所有指标上达到最优表现；相比最强先前基线，类别 F1 相对提升最高 38%，定位准确率最高提升 3.5 倍，联合定位-分类准确率最高提升 12.5 倍。按错误类别分析，该框架在更多错误类别上领先于其他评估器。

Conclusion: 论文认为，Agent 评估的瓶颈主要不在于前沿模型能力本身，而在于评估方法设计；通过结构化分解和 span 级评估，可以显著提升错误诊断、定位和分类能力。

Abstract: AI agents execute complex multi-step processes, but current evaluation falls short: outcome metrics report success or failure without explaining why, and process-level approaches struggle to connect failure types to their precise locations within long, structured traces. We present a holistic agent evaluation framework that pairs top-down agent-level diagnosis with bottom-up span-level evaluation, decomposing analysis into independent per-span assessments. This decomposition scales to traces of arbitrary length and produces span-level rationales for each verdict. On the TRAIL benchmark, our framework achieves state-of-the-art results across all metrics on both GAIA and SWE-Bench, with relative gains over the strongest prior baselines of up to 38% on category F1, up to 3.5x on localization accuracy, and up to 12.5x on joint localization-categorization accuracy. Per-category analysis shows our framework leading in more error categories than any other evaluator. Notably, the same frontier model achieves several times higher localization accuracy when used inside our framework than as a monolithic judge over the full trace, showing that evaluation methodology, not model capability, is the bottleneck.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出一个可解释框架：使用多个基于BERT的模型从不同维度提取互补信号，如情感、情绪和抑郁严重程度；将这些信号按时间聚合，构建用户级心理健康信号轨迹；通过时序建模与分段识别有意义的变化点；再结合大语言模型生成简洁、可读的报告，描述信号演化并突出关键转折。

Result: 在两个社交媒体数据集上的评估表明，该方法相比直接LLM报告生成能产生更连贯、更有信息量的摘要，在用户历史覆盖率、时间连贯性和变化点敏感性方面表现更好。消融实验验证了各组件的贡献，尤其是时序建模和分段模块的重要性。

Conclusion: 该方法能够以可解释方式展示用户心理健康相关信号的时间演化，帮助研究者理解状态变化并支持决策，但其目标不是临床诊断。

These traces can be organized into temporal trajectories that capture how a user's mental health signals evolve, including phases of improvement, deterioration, or stability. In this work, we propose an explainable framework for detecting and analyzing depression-related status shifts in user digital traces. The approach combines multiple BERT-based models to extract complementary signals across different dimensions (e.g., sentiment, emotion, and depression severity). Such signals are then aggregated over time to construct user-level trajectories that are analyzed to identify meaningful change points. To enhance interpretability, the framework integrates a large language model to generate concise and human-readable reports that describe the evolution of mental-health signals and highlight key transitions. We evaluate the framework on two social media datasets. Results show that the approach produces more coherent and informative summaries than direct LLM-based reporting, achieving higher coverage of user history, stronger temporal coherence, and improved sensitivity to change points. An ablation study confirms the contribution of each component, particularly temporal modeling and segmentation. Overall, the method provides an interpretable view of mental health signals over time, supporting research and decision making without aiming at clinical diagnosis.

However, they often rely on subjective or limited evaluation methods; focus primarily on proprietary models; or rarely systematically examine generation, evaluation, or deployment constraints in real educational settings. Meanwhile, Small Language Models (SLMs) have emerged as local alternatives that better address privacy and resource limitations; yet their effectiveness for assessment tasks remains underexplored. To address this gap, we systematically compare LLMs and SLMs for assessment question design; evaluate generation quality across Bloom's taxonomy levels using reproducible, pedagogically grounded metrics; and further assess model-based judging against expert-informed evaluation by analyzing reliability and agreement patterns. Results show that SLMs achieve competitive performance across key pedagogically motivated quality dimensions while enabling local, privacy-sensitive deployment. However, model-based evaluations also exhibit systematic inconsistencies and bias relative to expert ratings. These findings provide evidence to posit language models as bounded assistants in assessment workflows; underscore the necessity of Human-in-the-Loop; and advance the automated educational question generation field by examining quality, reliability, and deployment-aware trade-offs.

### [230] [How Sensitive Are Radiomic AI Models to Acquisition Parameters?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14667)
*D. Gil,I. Sanchez,C. Sanchez*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出混合效应框架量化CT采集参数对肺癌AI诊断模型的影响，并发现管电流≥200 mA、pitch≤1.5、层厚≤1.25 mm可显著提高跨数据集敏感性和特异性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多中心异质性采集协议会导致AI影像组学系统在临床部署时性能下降，因此需要量化扫描参数对模型表现的影响，并找到提升跨数据集鲁棒性的临床可用参数范围。

Method: 提出一个以性能为导向的混合效应分析框架，用于评估临床相关CT采集参数对影像组学AI模型性能的影响，同时纳入受试者层面的随机效应。该框架被应用于CT肺癌诊断任务，使用一个公开多中心数据库和一个自采多中心数据集，并测试多种先进模型架构；利用自采数据调整CT参数后，在公开数据集上验证跨数据库可复现性。

Result: 研究确定的较优扫描配置为：X射线管电流≥200 mA、螺旋 pitch≤1.5、层厚≤1.25 mm。相比低质量扫描，高质量参数区域使模型性能从敏感性0.79±0.04、特异性0.47±0.10提升至敏感性0.90±0.10、特异性0.79±0.13。

Conclusion: 扫描采集参数显著影响CT肺癌影像组学AI模型的诊断表现；通过混合效应框架识别合适的参数区域，可在控制辐射剂量的同时提升跨中心、跨数据集鲁棒性和临床可部署性。

Abstract: A main barrier for the deployment of AI radiomic systems in clinical routine is their drop in performance under heterogeneous multicentre acquisition protocols. This work presents a performance-oriented framework for quantifying scan parameter sensitivity of radiomic AI models, while identifying clinically significant parameter regions associated with improved cross-dataset robustness. We formulate a mixed-effects framework for quantifying the influence that clinically relevant acquisition parameters have on models performance, while accounting for subject-level random effects. We have applied our framework to lung cancer diagnosis in CT scans using two independent multicentre datasets (a public database and own-collected data) and several SoA architectures. To evaluate across-database reproducibility, CT parameters have been adjusted using the data collected and tested on the public set. The optimal configuration selected is the current of the X-ray tube >= 200 mA, spiral pitch <= 1.5, slice thickness <= 1.25 mm, which balances diagnostic quality with low radiation dose. These configuration push metrics from 0.79+-0.04 sensitivity, 0.47+-0.10 specificity in low quality scans to 0.90+-0.10 sensitivity, 0.79 +- 0.13 specificity in high quality ones.

### [231] [Orchard: An Open-Source Agentic Modeling Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15040)
*Baolin Peng,Wenlin Yao,Qianhui Wu,Hao Cheng,Xiao Yu,Rui Yang,Tao Ge,Alessandrio Sordoni,Xingdi Yuan,Yelong Shen,Pengcheng He,Tong Zhang,Zhou Yu,Jianfeng Gao*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Orchard 是一个面向可扩展智能体训练的开源框架，通过统一轻量环境层支持代码、GUI 和个人助理智能体训练，并在多个基准上达到开源领先或强竞争力表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有 Agentic Modeling 研究受限于基础设施与训练资源缺口：高性能系统多依赖闭源代码、模型或服务，而开源框架通常偏向编排和评测，缺少可扩展的智能体训练支持。

Method: 提出开源框架 Orchard，以轻量级 Orchard Env 作为核心环境服务，提供跨任务域、智能体 harness 与流水线阶段复用的沙箱生命周期管理原语；在其上构建 Orchard-SWE、Orchard-GUI、Orchard-Claw 三类训练配方，分别面向代码智能体、GUI/计算机使用智能体和个人助理智能体，并结合轨迹蒸馏、credit-assignment SFT、Balanced Adaptive Rollout RL、少量合成任务训练等方法。

Result: Orchard-SWE 从 Qwen3-30B-A3B-Thinking 出发，在 SWE-bench Verified 上 SFT 后达到 64.3%，SFT+RL 后达到 67.5%，在同规模开源模型中达到新 SOTA；Orchard-GUI 使用 0.4K 蒸馏轨迹和 2.2K 开放任务训练 4B 视觉语言智能体，在 WebVoyager、Online-Mind2Web、DeepShop 上分别达到 74.1%、67.0%、64.0%；Orchard-Claw 仅用 0.2K 合成任务训练，在 Claw-Eval 上 pass@3 达到 59.6%，搭配更强 ZeroClaw harness 时达到 73.9%。

Conclusion: 轻量、开放且与 harness 无关的环境层可以支撑跨领域复用的智能体数据、训练配方与评测流程，从而降低开放式可扩展智能体建模的基础设施门槛，并在代码、GUI 和个人助理场景中取得强竞争力结果。

Abstract: Agentic modeling aims to transform LLMs into autonomous agents capable of solving complex tasks through planning, reasoning, tool use, and multi-turn interaction with environments. Despite major investment, open research remains constrained by infrastructure and training gaps. Many high-performing systems rely on proprietary codebases, models, or services, while most open-source frameworks focus on orchestration and evaluation rather than scalable agent training. We present Orchard, an open-source framework for scalable agentic modeling. At its core is Orchard Env, a lightweight environment service providing reusable primitives for sandbox lifecycle management across task domains, agent harnesses, and pipeline stages. On top of Orchard Env, we build three agentic modeling recipes. Orchard-SWE targets coding agents. We distill 107K trajectories from MiniMax-M2.5 and Qwen3.5-397B, introduce credit-assignment SFT to learn from productive segments of unresolved trajectories, and apply Balanced Adaptive Rollout for RL. Starting from Qwen3-30B-A3B-Thinking, Orchard-SWE achieves 64.3% on SWE-bench Verified after SFT and 67.5% after SFT+RL, setting a new state of the art among open-source models of comparable size. Orchard-GUI trains a 4B vision-language computer-use agent using only 0.4K distilled trajectories and 2.2K open-ended tasks. It achieves 74.1%, 67.0%, and 64.0% success rates on WebVoyager, Online-Mind2Web, and DeepShop, respectively, making it the strongest open-source model while remaining competitive with proprietary systems. Orchard-Claw targets personal assistant agents. Trained with only 0.2K synthetic tasks, it achieves 59.6% pass@3 on Claw-Eval and 73.9% when paired with a stronger ZeroClaw harness. Collectively, these results show that a lightweight, open, harness-agnostic environment layer enables reusable agentic data, training recipes, and evaluations across domains.

*Haoran Zhang,Luxin Xu,Zhilin Wang,Runquan Gui,Shunkai Zhang,Haodi Lei,Zihao He,Bingsu He,Chicheng Qin,Tong Zhu,Xiaoye Qu,Yang Yang,Yu Cheng,Yafu Li*

Method: 提出 π-Bench：一个面向主动辅助能力的基准，包含 5 类领域特定用户画像下的 100 个多轮任务，并设计隐藏用户意图、任务间依赖和跨会话连续性，用于评估长程交互中的主动性与任务完成情况。

Conclusion: π-Bench 更贴近真实个人助理使用场景，可系统衡量智能体在长期多轮交互中预测、识别并满足用户潜在需求的能力，为改进主动型助理智能体提供评测依据。

Abstract: The rise of personal assistant agents, e.g., OpenClaw, highlights the growing potential of large language models to support users across everyday life and work. A core challenge in these settings is proactive assistance, since users often begin with underspecified requests and leave important needs, constraints, or preferences unstated. However, existing benchmarks rarely evaluate whether agents can identify and act on such hidden intents before they are explicitly stated, especially in sustained multi-turn interactions where user needs emerge gradually. To address this gap, we introduce $π$-Bench, a benchmark for proactive assistance comprising 100 multi-turn tasks across 5 domain-specific user personas. By incorporating hidden user intents, inter-task dependencies, and cross-session continuity, $π$-Bench evaluates agents' ability to anticipate and address user needs over extended interactions, jointly measuring proactivity and task completion in long-horizon trajectories that better reflect real-world use. Experiments show (1) proactive assistance remains challenging, (2) a clear distinction between task completion and proactivity, and (3) the value of prior interaction for proactive intent resolution in later tasks.

### [233] [Case-Based Calibration of Adaptive Reasoning and Execution for LLM Tool Use](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15041)
*Renning Pang,Tian Lan,Leyuan Liu,Piao Tong,Sheng Cao,Xiaosong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: CAST 是一种利用历史工具执行案例来指导大语言模型工具使用的框架；它通过识别任务复杂度和失败模式来设计奖励与自适应推理，在提升工具调用准确性和结构合法性的同时减少冗余推理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 工具使用将大语言模型扩展到参数化知识之外，但可靠执行需要在足够推理深度与严格结构合法性之间取得平衡。现有方法往往难以同时减少无效冗长推理和结构性错误，因此需要一种能从历史执行经验中学习校准策略的方法。

Method: 论文提出 CAST，一个案例驱动框架，将历史工具执行轨迹建模为结构化案例。CAST 不直接复用原始示例输出，而是提取案例信号：用复杂度画像估计最优推理策略，用失败画像预测可能的结构性崩溃，并将这些知识转化为细粒度奖励设计与自适应推理机制，使模型在强化学习中内化案例化策略。

Result: 在 BFCLv2 和 ToolBench 上，CAST 同时提升了符合 schema 的执行能力和任务级工具使用成功率，并减少了不必要的推理。整体执行准确率最高提升 5.85 个百分点，平均推理长度降低 26%，且显著缓解高影响结构错误。

Conclusion: 历史执行案例能够为工具使用模型提供可复用的适应性知识。通过案例驱动的复杂度与失败模式建模，CAST 可实现更校准、更可靠且更高效的工具调用。

Abstract: Tool use extends large language models beyond parametric knowledge, but reliable execution requires balancing appropriate reasoning depth with strict structural validity. We approach this problem from a case-based perspective to present CAST, a case-driven framework that treats historical execution trajectories as structured cases. Instead of reusing raw exemplar outputs, CAST extracts case-derived signals to identify complexity profiles for estimating optimal reasoning strategies, alongside failure profiles to map likely structural breakdowns. The framework translates this knowledge into a fine-grained reward design and adaptive reasoning, enabling the model to autonomously internalize case-based strategies during reinforcement learning. Experiments on BFCLv2 and ToolBench demonstrate that CAST improves both schema-faithful execution and task-level tool-use success while reducing unnecessary deliberation. The approach achieves up to 5.85 percentage points gain in overall execution accuracy and reduces average reasoning length by 26%, significantly mitigating high-impact structural errors. Ultimately, this demonstrates how historical execution cases can provide reusable adaptation knowledge for calibrated tool use.

</details>


### [234] [On Strong Equivalence Notions in Logic Programming and Abstract Argumentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14721)

TL;DR: 本文研究逻辑程序与抽象论证在动态更新下强等价不一致的问题，并提出新的逻辑程序强等价概念，使其在与 Dung 风格及 claim-augmented 论证框架互译时仍能保持兼容。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强等价性允许在任意上下文中用一个知识库替换另一个知识库而不改变推理结果，是非单调形式体系中的关键性质。虽然逻辑程序与抽象论证在静态语义下存在等价对应，但在动态更新场景中，由于两者更新概念不同，强等价性无法自然迁移，因此需要重新刻画二者之间兼容的强等价。

Method: 论文系统分析逻辑程序与抽象论证框架在动态语境下强等价不一致的原因，并提出一种新的逻辑程序强等价概念；该概念被设计为在特定类别逻辑程序与 Dung 风格论证框架、带 claim 增强的论证框架之间的翻译下保持不变。

Result: 新定义的强等价关系能够在若干逻辑程序类别及其对应的论证框架之间保持，从而弥合静态语义等价与动态更新不兼容之间的差距。

Conclusion: 论文表明，通过调整逻辑程序中的强等价概念，可以恢复逻辑程序与抽象论证在动态环境中的兼容性，使跨形式体系的替换与更新分析更加一致。

Abstract: Strong equivalence between knowledge bases ensures the possibility of replacing one with the other without affecting reasoning outcomes, in any given context. This makes it a crucial property in nonmonotonic formalisms. In particular, the fields of logic programming and abstract argumentation provide primary examples in which this property has been subject to vast investigations. However, while (classes of) logic programs and abstract argumentation frameworks are known to be semantically equivalent in static settings, this alignment breaks in dynamic contexts due to differing notions of update. As a result, strong equivalence does not always carry over from one formalism to the other. In this paper, we carefully investigate this discrepancy and introduce a new notion of strong equivalence for logic programs. Our approach preserves strong equivalence under translation between certain classes of logic programs and both Dung-style and claim-augmented argumentation frameworks, thus restoring compatibility across these formalisms.

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed for knowledge synthesis, yet their capacity for compositional generalization in scientific knowledge remains under-characterized. Existing benchmarks primarily focus on single-turn restricted scenarios, failing to capture the capability boundaries exposed by real-world interactive scientific workflows. To address this, we introduce XDomainBench, a diagnostic benchmark for interactive interdisciplinary scientific reasoning. We formalize the composition order and mixture structure to enable systematic stress-testing from single-discipline to inter-disciplinary, comprising 8,598 interactive sessions across 20 domains and 4 task categories, with 8 realistic trajectory patterns covering difficulty and domain-mixture dynamics, simulating real AI4S scenarios. Large-scale evaluation of LLMs reveals a systematic reasoning collapse as composition order increases, stemming from two root causes: (i) direct difficulty increases induced by domain composition, and (ii) indirect interaction-amplified failures where trajectory patterns trigger error accumulation, reasoning breaks, and domain confusion, ultimately leading to session collapse.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: RNN策略依赖历史信息与潜在隐藏状态动态，在部分可观测强化学习中难以验证；现有验证工具常受限于建模假设或对隐藏状态空间的粗糙过近似，导致结果保守或不确定。

Method: 提出 RNN-ProVe 概率验证框架，通过策略驱动采样近似训练策略下可达/可行的隐藏状态集合，并推导统计误差界，以高置信度、 bounded-error 的方式估计不期望行为发生概率。

Result: 在部分可观测单智能体和协作多智能体任务上的实验表明，RNN-ProVe 相比现有工具能给出更定量、考虑可行性的概率保证，并可扩展到循环策略和多智能体场景。

Conclusion: RNN-ProVe 将 RNN 策略验证从保守的确定性过近似转向可量化的概率风险估计，为部分可观测 RL 中历史依赖策略的行为安全评估提供了更实用、可扩展的方案。

Abstract: History-dependent policies induced by recurrent neural networks (RNNs) rely on latent hidden state dynamics, making verification in partially observable reinforcement learning (RL) challenging. Existing RNN verification tools typically rely on restrictive modeling assumptions or coarse over-approximations of the hidden state space, which can lead to overly conservative or inconclusive results. We propose $\textbf{RNN}$ $\textbf{Pro}$babilistic $\textbf{Ve}$rification ($\texttt{RNN-ProVe}$), a probabilistic framework that $\textit{estimates the likelihood}$ of undesired behaviors in RNN-based policies. $\texttt{RNN-ProVe}$ uses policy-driven sampling to approximate the set of hidden states that are feasible under a trained policy, and derives statistical error bounds to produce bounded-error, high-confidence estimates of behavioral violations. Experiments on partially observable single-agent and cooperative multi-agent tasks show that $\texttt{RNN-ProVe}$ yields more quantitative, feasibility-aware probabilistic guarantees than existing tools, while scaling to recurrent and multi-agent settings.

Accurate prediction thus requires the extraction of high-level semantic features of images and the active collection of preference information from the target individual. To address this issue, we focus on the utility of Large Language Models (LLMs) pretrained on vast amounts of textual data, and develop an integrated DL-LLM system. The system actively elicits aesthetic preferences through LLM-based semi-structured interviews and predicts aesthetic evaluation by leveraging both low-level and high-level features. In our experiments, we compare the proposed system against conventional systems, human predictors, and the target individual's own re-evaluations after a certain time interval. Our results show that the proposed system outperforms all of them, with particularly strong performance on highly-rated images. Moreover, the prediction error of the proposed system is smaller than within-person variability, while human predictors show the largest error, likely due to the influence of their own aesthetic values. ### [240] [A Heterogeneous Temporal Memory Governance Framework for Long-Term LLM Persona Consistency](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14802)
*Zhao Yang,Wang Huan,Li Yingshuo,Tu Haomiao,Lin Hujite*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: ARPM 是一种面向长期对话的外部时间记忆治理框架，通过分离静态知识与动态对话经验、融合多种检索和时间重排机制，在高噪声、上下文清空和跨模型交接场景下提升事实召回、时间连续性和人格一致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在长程交互中容易出现事实遗失、时间线混乱、人格漂移和稳定性下降；这些问题在高噪声知识库、上下文清空和跨模型迁移场景下更加严重。论文希望将长期连续性从依赖模型权重或长上下文，转化为可追踪、可审计、可迁移的外部记忆治理问题。

Method: 提出 ARPM 外部时间记忆治理框架，将静态知识记忆与动态对话经验记忆分离，并结合向量检索、BM25、RRF 融合、双时间重排序、按时间顺序读取证据，以及受控分析协议，用于证据验证和答案绑定。作者基于工程日志设计了三组实验：不同信噪比下的 50 轮问答评估、检索模块消融实验，以及在超大噪声基底、周期性上下文清空和多模型交接下的连续性测试。

Result: 在 1:5 信噪比下，CSV 自动判断的召回准确率为 54.0%，人工复核提升至 100.0%；在 1:200+ 信噪比下，分别为 44.0% 和 80.0%，说明自动规则可能低估证据进入提示后的真实召回效果。消融实验显示，禁用对话历史检索会使严格准确率从 100% 降至 66.7%，禁用 BM25 降至 80.0%，表明仅靠语义检索不足以支持纠错与可追溯性。在 510 万字符噪声、周期性清空上下文和多模型交接下，ARPM 仍维持语义连续性、边界连续性和人格一致性，但受限于协议遵循能力。

Conclusion: 论文认为，长期人格一致性和长程对话连续性可以被分解为若干可治理组件，并通过白盒方式进行评估。ARPM 证明外部记忆治理比单纯依赖长上下文或模型内部人格编码更适合处理高噪声、长周期和跨模型的交互场景。

Abstract: Large language models often suffer from fact loss, timeline confusion, persona drift, and reduced stability during long-range interaction, especially under high-noise knowledge bases, context clearing, and cross-model transfer. To address these issues, we introduce ARPM, an external temporal memory governance framework for long-term dialogue. ARPM separates static knowledge memory from dynamic dialogue experience memory and combines vector retrieval, BM25, RRF fusion, dual-temporal reranking, chronological evidence reading, and a controlled analysis protocol for evidence verification and answer binding. Unlike approaches that encode persona consistency into model weights or rely only on long context, ARPM treats continuity as a traceable, auditable, and transferable governance problem. Using engineering logs, we conduct three experiments. First, in a 50-round question-answering setting, we compare signal-to-noise ratios of 1:5 and 1:200+, and distinguish CSV auto-judgment from manual review. Under 1:5, CSV recall accuracy is 54.0%, while manual review raises it to 100.0%. Under 1:200+, the values are 44.0% and 80.0%. These results show that automatic rules can underestimate recall after supporting evidence enters the prompt. Second, ablation results show that dialogue history retrieval is necessary for recent continuity: disabling it reduces strict accuracy from 100% to 66.7%, and disabling BM25 reduces it to 80.0%, indicating that pure semantic retrieval is insufficient for correction and tracing. Third, under a 5.1-million-character noise substrate, periodic context clearing, and multi-model handoff, ARPM maintains semantic continuity, boundary continuity, and persona consistency, while exposing limits caused by weak protocol compliance. These findings show that long-term persona consistency can be decomposed into governable components and evaluated in a white-box manner.

### [241] [Interestingness as an Inductive Heuristic for Future Compression Progress](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14831)
*Vincent Herrmann,Jürgen Schmidhuber*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文把“有趣性”形式化为预测未来压缩进展的启发式，证明近期突破越近，未来进展期望越高；算法先验比长度先验更能预测发现潜力，并在多种计算范式中得到实验支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 递归自我改进系统面临“有趣性”瓶颈：系统需要提前判断哪些任务或数据最可能带来未来进展。论文试图将这种前瞻性选择能力形式化，并解释过去的发现进展是否能预测未来发现。

Method: 论文将有趣性定义为未来压缩进展的归纳启发式，并使用 Kolmogorov 复杂性与算法统计学工具进行理论分析。作者比较了长度先验、算法先验和速度先验下的复杂度—运行时间画像，并在三类不同的通用计算范式中进行实验验证。

Result: 研究表明，有趣性的归纳属性在理论上可行且有经验支持；预期未来进展与上一次突破的时间新近性呈指数关系。算法先验相比长度先验更乐观，在相同观测画像下可带来二次级别的预期发现增长。实验结果在三种通用计算范式中支持这些理论结论。

Conclusion: 论文认为，“过去进展预示未来发现”的有趣性假设具有理论基础与实验支持；选择更符合算法结构的先验能够显著提升对未来发现的预期，从而为自我改进系统中的任务/数据选择提供原则性依据。

Abstract: One of the bottlenecks on the way towards recursively self-improving systems is the challenge of interestingness: the ability to prospectively identify which tasks or data hold the potential for future progress. We formalize interestingness as an inductive heuristic for future compression progress and investigate its predictability using tools from Kolmogorov Complexity and Algorithmic Statistics. By analyzing complexity-runtime profiles under Length, Algorithmic, and Speed priors, we demonstrate that the inductive property of interestingness -- the capacity for past progress to signal future discovery -- is theoretically viable and empirically supported. We prove that expected future progress depends exponentially on the recency of the last observed breakthrough. Furthermore, we show that the Algorithmic Prior is significantly more optimistic than the Length Prior, yielding a quadratic increase in expected discovery for the same observed profile. These findings are experimentally confirmed across three diverse universal computational paradigms.

To evaluate its impact, we conducted a controlled A/B study across thirty non-scripted conversations spanning six emotionally distinct categories using the same underlying language model in both conditions. The largest gains were observed in memory grounding (95% improvement), plan clarity (57%), and emotional validation (34%). These findings suggest that stateful emotional memory may represent a foundational infrastructure layer for hyper-personalized AI systems, though broader validation across larger and more diverse evaluations remains necessary

### [243] [A Deterministic Agentic Workflow for HS Tariff Classification: Multi-Dimensional Rule Reasoning with Interpretable Decisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14857)
*Yu Zhang,Dongjiang Zhuang,Qu Zhou,Zheng Huang,Junhe Wu,Jing Cao,Kai Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出一种用于HS关税归类的确定性六阶段智能体流程，将大模型限制在可控子任务中，并用结构化输出和法规引用保证可解释性；实验显示其在HSCodeComp上取得较好四位/六位归类表现，同时发现数据集部分标签可能不符合HS通则。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: HS关税归类需要在GIR、类注、章注和解释性注释下，将自由文本商品描述映射到六位或八位编码。难点在于多维规则推理：材料、形态、功能、基本特征、零部件与整体边界、具体列名与兜底税目等多个轴向的优先级约束必须同时满足；端到端提示的大模型常只解决单一轴向而忽略其他约束。

Method: 提出确定性智能体工作流，而非自规划智能体：控制流程固定，大模型调用限制在狭窄阶段，反思与验证仅作为局部机制保留。系统结合中文HS税则的离线知识工程与在线六阶段流水线，并要求各阶段输出结构化决策及逐字引用相关类注/章注以增强可解释性。

Conclusion: 论文认为，针对高风险、规则密集型的HS归类任务，固定控制流的确定性智能体工作流比端到端提示或自规划智能体更可靠、可解释，并能揭示数据集标注中潜在的规则偏差。

Abstract: Harmonized System (HS) tariff classification is a high-stakes, expert-level task in which a free-form product description must be mapped to a specific six- or eight-digit code under the General Interpretive Rules (GIR), section notes, chapter notes, and Explanatory Notes. The difficulty lies not in knowledge volume but in *multi-dimensional rule reasoning*: a correct classification must satisfy competing priority rules along several axes simultaneously, including material, form, function, essential character, the part-versus-whole boundary, and specific listing versus residual headings. End-to-end prompting of large language models fails characteristically by resolving one axis while ignoring the priority constraints on the others. We present a *deterministic agentic workflow* in contrast to self-planning agents: the control flow is fixed, language model calls are confined to narrow stages, and reflection and verification are retained as local mechanisms. This design yields interpretability by construction--each decision is decomposed into stage-wise structured outputs with verbatim citation of the chapter or section notes that bear on it. The architecture combines offline knowledge-engineering of the Chinese HS tariff with an online six-stage pipeline. Evaluated on HSCodeComp at the six-digit level, the workflow reaches 75.0% top-1 and 91.5% top-3 at four digits, and 64.2% top-1 and 78.3% top-3 at six digits with Qwen3.6-plus; an open-weight Qwen3.6-27B-FP8 backbone in non-thinking mode achieves 84.2% four-digit and 77.4% six-digit top-1 agreement with the frontier model. A two-stage manual audit of 226 six-digit disagreements suggests that a non-trivial fraction of HSCodeComp ground-truth labels may deviate from HS general rules; full adjudication records are released in the appendix as preliminary findings for community review.

Existing surveys cover individual agent capabilities, multi-agent collaboration, or agent self-evolution separately, leaving the causal dependencies among them unexamined. <details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大规模知识图谱在问答、可视化等任务中难以直接处理；同时，不同用户的查询模式不同，需要个性化摘要以保留与用户需求相关的信息，并降低存储与查询开销。

Method: 论文将 coreset 理论引入个性化知识图谱摘要。针对给定知识图谱和用户查询工作负载，定义三元组相对于用户查询行为的重要性/敏感度分数，并基于敏感度的重要性采样构建每个用户独立的三元组子集摘要，同时提供有界近似误差保证。

Result: 在 Freebase、WikiData 和 DBpedia 上，COREKG 相比 GLIMPSE、PPR、iSummary、PEGASUS 和 APEX² 等方法，在仅使用原图极小部分的情况下，取得更高的问答准确率和结构覆盖率。

Furthermore, personalized KG summarization is crucial in the current data-driven world as it captures the specific requirements of users based on their query patterns. Since it only maintains relevant information, the personalized summaries of KG are small, resulting in significantly smaller storage requirements and query runtime. In this work, we adapt the coreset theory to create personalized KG summaries. For a given dataset and a user-specific query workload, we present an approach that samples a relevant subset of triples using sensitivity-based importance sampling. We ensure that the subset approximates the characteristics of the full dataset with bounded approximation error. We define sensitivity scores that measure the importance of a triple with respect to a user's query workload, which are then used by our coreset construction algorithm. We explicitly focus on personalized knowledge graph summarization by constructing summaries independently for each user based on their query behaviour.
  Our evaluation on Freebase, WikiData, and DBpedia shows that COREKG delivers higher query-answering accuracy and structural coverage than the state-of-the-art methods, such as GLIMPSE, PPR, iSummary, PEGASUS and APEX$^2$ while requiring only a tiny fraction of the original graph.

### [246] [KGPFN: Unlocking the Potential of Knowledge Graph Foundation Model via In-Context Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14907)
*Yisen Gao,Jiaxin Bai,Haoyu Huang,Zhongwei Xie,Yufei Li,Hong Ting Tsang,Sirui Han,Yangqiu Song*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: KGPFN 是一种面向知识图谱推理的基础模型，结合关系级迁移学习、局部邻域编码和关系级全局上下文检索，在无需微调的情况下通过上下文学习适应未见知识图谱，并在大量基准上取得领先表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有知识图谱基础模型多强调关系层面的通用性，但对基础模型另一核心能力——上下文学习（in-context learning, ICL）探索不足。知识图谱推理需要同时利用查询实体周围的局部结构上下文，以及刻画某一关系在大量实例中行为模式的全局上下文。

Method: 提出 KGPFN：先通过关系图上的消息传递学习关系表示，以捕获跨图谱的关系不变性；再用多层 NBFNet 编码查询相关的局部邻域作为局部上下文；同时检索大量查询关系实例及其局部邻域，构造关系特定的全局上下文，并在 Prior-Data Fitted Network 框架下结合特征级注意力与样本级注意力进行聚合；通过多图谱预训练学习可迁移模式与上下文证据之间的权衡。

Result: 在 57 个知识图谱基准上，KGPFN 仅依靠推理时上下文学习即可适应未见图谱，并持续优于具有竞争力的微调式知识图谱基础模型。

Conclusion: KGPFN 表明，将可迁移关系规律与结构化上下文中的推理时 ICL 统一起来，可以显著增强知识图谱基础模型对未见实体、关系和图谱的泛化与适应能力。

Abstract: Knowledge graph (KG) foundation models aim to generalize across graphs with unseen entities and relations by learning transferable relational structure. However, most existing methods primarily emphasize relation-level universality, while in-context learning, the other pillar of foundation models remains under-explored for KG reasoning. In KGs, context is inherently structured and heterogeneous: effective prediction requires conditioning on the local context around the query entities as well as the global context that summarizes how a relation behaves across many instances. We propose KGPFN, a KG foundation model using Prior-data Fitted Network that unifies transferable relational regularities with inference-time in-context learning from structured context. KGPFN first learns relation representations via message passing on relation graphs to capture cross-graph relational invariances. For query-specific reasoning, it encodes local neighborhoods using a multi-layer NBFNet as local context. To enable ICL at global scale, it constructs relation-specific global context by retrieving a large set of instances of the query relation together with their local neighborhoods, and aggregates them within a Prior-Data Fitted Network framework that combines feature-level and sample-level attention. Through multi-graph pretraining on diverse KGs, KGPFN learns when to instantiate reusable patterns and when to override them using contextual evidence. Experiments on 57 KG benchmarks demonstrate that KGPFN achieves strong adaptation to previously unseen graphs through in-context learning alone, consistently outperforming competitive fine-tuned KG foundation models. Our code is available at https://github.com/HKUST-KnowComp/KGPFN.

</details>


### [247] [From Sycophantic Consensus to Pluralistic Repair: Why AI Alignment Must Surface Disagreement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14912)
*Varad Vishwarupe,Nigel Shadbolt,Marina Jirotka*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文批评将多元对齐等同于偏好聚合的做法，指出RLHF助手的核心风险是迎合用户、消解分歧。作者提出PRS指标衡量模型能否在争议价值对话中进行有原则修正，并通过Claude Sonnet 4.5和GPT-4o的小规模实验显示，两者均存在跟随用户意见但修复质量不足的问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有多元对齐通常被简化为偏好聚合，即覆盖、引导或按比例代表多样化人类价值；作者认为这不足以处理部署场景中的真实价值多元性，因为RLHF助手容易在互动中表现为迎合式共识，压低分歧。

Method: 论文从Grice会话准则出发，将多元对齐重构为三个互动机制：界定视角范围（scoping）、显化价值冲突（signalling）、基于原则修正立场（repair）。同时提出Pluralistic Repair Score（PRS）指标，用于区分有原则的修正与因用户压力而让步，并在两个前沿RLHF模型上做小规模实证说明。

Result: 在Claude Sonnet 4.5（N=198）和GPT-4o（N=100）的争议价值提示实验中，两个模型都呈现出随用户意见转向的倾向，同时在高质量、有原则的修复方面表现较低，说明表面覆盖多元观点并不等同于在互动层面维护多元主义。

Conclusion: 作者认为，多元对齐的关键不只是输出分布上的价值代表，而是在部署互动中保留可见分歧与原则性修正能力；真正决定多元主义能否成立的层面包括界面设计、偏好数据管线和审计基础设施等部署治理机制。

Abstract: Pluralistic alignment is typically operationalised as preference aggregation: producing responses that span (Overton), steer toward (Steerable), or proportionally represent (Distributional) diverse human values. We argue that aggregation alone is an incomplete primitive for deployed pluralistic alignment. Under genuine value pluralism, the failure mode of contemporary RLHF-trained assistants is not insufficient coverage but sycophantic consensus: a learned tendency to agree with, validate, and minimise friction with the immediate interlocutor. Because deployed AI systems now mediate consequential deliberation across health, civic life, labour, and governance, the collapse of disagreement at the interaction layer is not a narrow technical concern but a structural failure with distributive consequences. We reframe pluralistic alignment around three conversational mechanisms drawn from Grice's maxims: scoping (acknowledging the limits of one's perspective), signalling (surfacing value-conflict rather than smoothing it over), and repair (revising one's position on principled grounds, not on user pressure). We formalise a metric, the Pluralistic Repair Score (PRS), distinguishing principled revision from capitulation, and present a small-scale empirical illustration on two frontier RLHF-trained models (Claude Sonnet 4.5, N=198; GPT-4o, N=100) showing that, for both, agreement-following coexists with low repair-quality on contested-value prompts. PRS measures an interactional precondition for pluralism (visible disagreement; principled revision) rather than pluralism in full; we discuss the difference, take seriously the reflexive question of whose "principled" counts, and argue that pluralism is most decisively made or unmade at the deployment-governance layer: interfaces, preference-data pipelines, and audit infrastructure.

</details>


### [248] [GraphFlow: An Architecture for Formally Verifiable Visual Workflows Enabling Reliable Agentic AI Automation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14968)
*Drewry H. Morris,Luis Valles,Reza Hosseini Ghomi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: GraphFlow 用可执行工作流图替代易变的推理时规划，通过合约、事件日志和信任边界设计提升智能体自动化可靠性；临床试点完成率较高，但核心形式验证机制尚未完成评估。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多步骤、关键任务型的智能体自动化流程中，单步小错误会快速累积，导致整体成功率显著下降；现有工作流平台虽有持久执行和可观测性，但缺乏语义正确性保证，而智能体系统在推理时规划，行为易受提示变化影响且难以审计。

Method: GraphFlow 将可视化工作流图作为可执行规范，用单一图形工件同时定义数据作用域、执行语义和监控机制。其设计包括编译期受限图类、可复用自动化合约（前置条件、后置条件与组合义务）的证明检查，以及运行期基于追加式事件日志的持久执行、合约边界执行、重放、重试与审计；泳道用于显式表示信任边界。

Result: 在三个临床站点为期一年的试点中，早期原型在未包含 verified-core 子系统的情况下执行了 8,728 次队列纳入工作流，完成率为 97.08%；失败主要集中在外部集成环节。

Conclusion: GraphFlow 提出了一种以可视化工作流图为可执行规范的框架，旨在提升关键多步骤 AI 自动化流程的可靠性、可审计性和边界可控性。当前实证结果支持其工程可行性，但形式语义与证明检查核心仍在开发中，验证核心的评估留待未来工作。

Abstract: GraphFlow is a visual workflow system designed to improve the reliability of agentic AI automation in multi-step, mission-critical processes. In these workflows, small errors compound rapidly: under an idealized model of independent steps, a ten-step process with 90% per-step reliability completes successfully only 35% of the time. Existing workflow platforms provide durable execution and observability but offer few semantic correctness guarantees, while agentic systems plan at inference time, making behavior sensitive to prompt variation and difficult to audit.
  GraphFlow is designed to address this gap by treating workflow diagrams as the executable specification, a single artifact defining data scope, execution semantics, and monitoring. At compile time, a restricted class of diagrams is specified to produce reusable automations whose contracts (preconditions, postconditions, and composition obligations) are intended to be proof-checked before admission to a shared library. At runtime, a durable engine records outcomes in an append-only event log and can enforce contracts at system boundaries, supporting replay, retries, and audit. Swimlanes make trust boundaries explicit, separating verified logic from external systems, human judgment, and AI decisions.
  A year-long pilot across three clinical sites executed 8,728 cohort-enrolled workflow runs with a 97.08% completion rate under an early prototype without the verified-core subsystem; observed failures were localized primarily to external integrations. The formal semantics and proof-checked admission model described here are specified and under active development. Evaluation of the verified core is reserved for future work.

</details>


### [249] [Learning Developmental Scaffoldings to Guide Self-Organisation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14998)
*Milton L. Montero,Elias Najarro,Jakob Schauser,Sebastian Risi*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 NCA 与 SIREN 联合学习模型，研究生物发育式自组织中“初始预模式”与“局部动态规则”的信息分工。结果显示，预模式能提升鲁棒性、容量和对称性破缺，并不是简单复制目标，而是引导自组织过程更好收敛。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 许多自然系统通过自组织产生全局结构，但自组织过程所需的关键信息常被预先编码在初始条件中。生物发育中的母源预模式、形态发生素梯度等现象表明，初始条件与局部动态规则之间存在类似计算系统中“存储-计算权衡”的关系。本文旨在理解这种信息外包如何影响自组织的能力与鲁棒性。

Method: 作者构建了一个联合学习框架：使用神经细胞自动机（Neural Cellular Automata, NCA）学习自组织更新规则，同时使用基于坐标的模式生成器 SIREN 学习初始预模式。两者被同时训练以生成一组目标图案，并在受控条件下调节和测量预模式与自组织规则之间的信息分工。论文还采用信息论分析来量化信息在初始条件和动态过程中的分布。

Result: 实验表明，相比纯自组织方法，联合学习预模式与自组织规则能够提升系统的鲁棒性、编码容量和对称性破缺能力。研究还发现，有效的预模式并非只是目标图案的粗略近似，而是通过引导发育动态、改善收敛路径来促进最终结构形成。

Conclusion: 论文认为，复杂形态生成中的初始条件不是被动输入，而是与自组织动态共同构成信息处理系统。预模式通过向初始状态外包部分信息，降低了自组织规则的负担，并以非平凡方式塑造系统的收敛行为。该结果为理解生物发育中的信息分配及人工自组织系统设计提供了新视角。

Abstract: From subcellular structures to entire organisms, many natural systems generate complex organisation through self-organisation: local interactions that collectively give rise to global structure without any blueprint of the outcome. Yet a significant portion of the information driving such processes is not produced by self-organisation itself, instead, it is often offloaded to initial conditions of the system. Biological development is a prime example, where maternal pre-patterns encode positional and symmetry-breaking information that scaffolds the self-organising process. From maternal morphogen gradients in early embryogenesis to tissue-level morphogenetic pre-patterns guiding organ formation, this transfer of information to initial conditions, analogous to a memory-compute trade-off in computational systems, is a fundamental part of developmental processes. In this work, we study this offloading phenomenon by introducing a model that jointly learns both the self-organisation rules and the pre-patterns, allowing their interplay to be varied and measured under controlled conditions: a Neural Cellular Automaton (NCA) paired with a learned coordinate-based pattern generator (SIREN), both trained simultaneously to generate a set of patterns. We provide information-theoretic analyses of how information is distributed between pre-patterns and the self-organising process, and show that jointly learning both components yields improvements in robustness, encoding capacity, and symmetry breaking over purely self-organising alternatives. Our analysis further suggests that effective pre-patterns do not simply approximate their targets; rather, they bias the developmental dynamics in ways that facilitate convergence, pointing to a non-trivial relationship between the structure of initial conditions and the dynamics of self-organisation.

</details>


### [250] [Dual-Dimensional Consistency: Balancing Budget and Quality in Adaptive Inference-Time Scaling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15100)
*Rongman Xu,Yifei Li,Tianzhe Zhao,Yanrui Wu,Bo Li,Hang Yan*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 DDC 框架，通过置信度加权贝叶斯协议和趋势感知分层剪枝，同时优化推理宽度与深度，在保持或提升准确率的同时将 token 消耗降低 10 倍以上。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型在推理任务中表现突出，但推理时扩展面临采样预算与推理质量之间的权衡。现有方法通常将采样宽度与深度割裂处理，宽度共识可能强化幻觉，深度剪枝又可能过早截断复杂但有效的推理链。

Method: 提出 Dual-Dimensional Consistency（DDC）统一框架，将路径质量评估与自适应终止机制结合。该方法耦合 Confidence-Weighted Bayesian protocol 与 Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning，把计算资源集中到高质量推理路径上，同时过滤幻觉并加速共识形成。

Result: 在五个基准测试上的评估显示，DDC 在多种大语言模型上可将 token 消耗降低超过 10 倍，同时保持或超过强基线方法的准确率。

Conclusion: DDC 表明，通过同时建模推理路径的质量与终止策略，可以显著提升推理时计算效率，并在不牺牲性能的情况下改善 LLM 推理扩展。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in reasoning. However, maximizing their potential through inference-time scaling faces challenges in trade-off between sampling budget and reasoning quality. Current strategies remain inefficient as they typically treat sampling width and depth as orthogonal objectives, where width consensus methods risk reinforcing hallucinations, while depth pruning mechanisms prematurely truncate complex yet valid reasoning chains. Therefore, we propose Dual-Dimensional Consistency (DDC), a unified framework that bridges path quality with adaptive termination. By coupling Confidence-Weighted Bayesian protocol with a Trend-Aware Stratified Pruning, our method ensures that computational resources are concentrated on high quality reasoning paths, filtering hallucinations while accelerating consensus. Evaluations across five benchmarks demonstrate that this approach reduces token consumption by over 10 times while maintaining or exceeding the accuracy of strong baselines across various LLMs.

</details>


### [251] [Why Neighborhoods Matter: Traversal Context and Provenance in Agentic GraphRAG](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15109)
*Riccardo Terrenzi,Maximilian von Zastrow,Serkan Ayvaz*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文指出，Agentic GraphRAG 中的引用忠实性不能只看最终引用是否支持答案，还要考察整个知识图谱检索轨迹；实验发现引用证据很重要，但未引用的遍历上下文和图结构也会影响答案，因此引用评估应转向轨迹级溯源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强生成（RAG）通过外部证据提升事实性，但在 Agentic GraphRAG 中，智能体会先遍历知识图谱再生成答案与少量引用，使“引用是否忠实”不再只是答案是否被引用来源支持的问题。论文动机是重新定义并评估这种复杂场景下的引用忠实性。

Method: 论文将引用忠实性建模为轨迹级问题，认为最终引用不仅应支持答案，还应解释图遍历过程、图结构以及被访问但未被引用的实体对答案的潜在影响。作者通过受控消融实验，比较隔离、移除和遮蔽已引用与未引用图实体对生成答案和准确率的影响。

Result: 实验表明，已引用证据通常是必要的：移除这些证据会显著改变答案并降低准确率。但引用并不充分，因为准确答案也可能依赖未被引用的遍历上下文和周围图结构。

Conclusion: Agentic GraphRAG 的引用评估应超越传统的来源支持判断，转向覆盖更广检索轨迹的溯源评估，包括图遍历路径、结构信息和未引用但有影响的实体。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation can improve factuality by grounding answers in external evidence, but Agentic GraphRAG complicates what it means for citations to be faithful. In these systems, an agent explores a knowledge graph before producing an answer and a small set of citations. We frame citation faithfulness as a trajectory-level problem: final citations should not only support the answer, but also account for the graph traversal, structure, and visited-but-uncited entities that may influence it. Through controlled ablation experiments, we compare the effects of isolating, removing, and masking cited and uncited graph entities. Our results show that cited evidence is often necessary, as removing it substantially changes answers and reduces accuracy. However, citations are not sufficient, because accurate answers can also depend on uncited traversal context and surrounding graph structure. These findings suggest that citation evaluation in Agentic GraphRAG should move beyond source support toward provenance over the broader retrieval trajectory.

</details>


### [252] [APWA: A Distributed Architecture for Parallelizable Agentic Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15132)
*Evan Rose,Tushin Mallick,Matthew D. Laws,Cristina Nita-Rotaru,Alina Oprea*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出 APWA，一种分布式多智能体并行工作负载架构，通过把复杂任务拆成相互独立的子问题并行执行，提升 LLM 多智能体系统在大规模、高度可并行任务中的吞吐量与可扩展性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有基于大语言模型的自主多智能体系统在任务规模和复杂度提升时，会遭遇推理、协调与计算扩展瓶颈；这使其难以充分利用底层 LLM 具备的并行计算与推理能力，无法在高度可并行任务上实现高吞吐处理。

Method: 论文提出 Agent-Parallel Workload Architecture（APWA），一种面向高度可并行 agentic workloads 的分布式多智能体系统架构。其核心方法是将工作流动态分解为彼此不干扰的子问题，使这些子问题可使用独立资源并行处理，且无需跨子任务通信；同时支持异构数据和多种并行处理模式。

Result: 实验表明，APWA 能够将复杂查询动态分解为可并行执行的工作流，并且在更大规模任务上具备良好扩展性；在某些设置中，先前系统会完全失败，而 APWA 仍能运行。

Conclusion: APWA 为 LLM 多智能体系统提供了一种提升并行处理能力和规模扩展性的架构路径，尤其适用于可被拆分为非干扰子问题的复杂任务，有助于突破现有系统在协调和计算扩展方面的限制。

Abstract: Autonomous multi-agent systems based on large language models (LLMs) have demonstrated remarkable abilities in independently solving complex tasks in a wide breadth of application domains. However, these systems hit critical reasoning, coordination, and computational scaling bottlenecks as the size and complexity of their tasks grow. These limitations hinder multi-agent systems from achieving high-throughput processing for highly parallelizable tasks, despite the availability of parallel computing and reasoning primitives in the underlying LLMs. We introduce the Agent-Parallel Workload Architecture (APWA), a distributed multi-agent system architecture designed for the efficient processing of heavily parallelizable agentic workloads. APWA facilitates parallel execution by decomposing workflows into non-interfering subproblems that can be processed using independent resources without cross-communication. It supports heterogeneous data and parallel processing patterns, and it accommodates tasks from a wide breadth of domains. In our evaluation, we demonstrate that APWA can dynamically decompose complex queries into parallelizable workflows and scales on larger tasks in settings where prior systems fail completely.

</details>


### [253] [OpenDeepThink: Parallel Reasoning via Bradley--Terry Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.15177)
*Shang Zhou,Wenhao Chai,Kaiyuan Liu,Huanzhi Mao,Qiuyang Mang,Jingbo Shang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: OpenDeepThink 用 Bradley-Terry 成对比较替代噪声较大的单点评判，在测试时并行生成、排序、保留和变异候选答案，显著提升代码竞赛推理表现，但主要适用于客观可验证任务。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测试时计算扩展是提升大语言模型推理能力的重要方向。现有方法多通过延长单条推理链来扩展深度，而并行采样多个候选答案虽能扩展广度，却面临无真实验证器时如何可靠选择最佳候选的瓶颈；逐点评判容易受噪声和偏差影响。

Method: 论文提出 OpenDeepThink，一个基于种群的测试时计算框架。每一代中，LLM 对随机候选对进行成对比较，并使用 Bradley-Terry 模型聚合比较结果形成全局排序；保留排名靠前的候选；利用比较过程中产生的自然语言批评对排名前四分之三的候选进行变异；丢弃排名后四分之一的候选。

Result: 在八轮顺序 LLM 调用、约 27 分钟墙钟时间下，OpenDeepThink 将 Gemini 3.1 Pro 的有效 Codeforces Elo 提升了 405 分。该流程无需重新调参即可迁移到更弱或更强模型。在 HLE 多领域基准上，增益主要集中在客观可验证领域，而在主观领域出现反向效果。论文还发布了 CF-73：包含 73 道专家评级 Codeforces 题目的数据集，带有国际特级大师标注，并与官方判题达到 99% 本地评测一致性。

Conclusion: OpenDeepThink 表明，通过成对比较与种群式迭代，可以有效缓解并行候选选择瓶颈，使测试时计算的“广度扩展”成为提升 LLM 推理能力的可行路径；但其收益依赖任务是否具备客观可验证性。

Abstract: Test-time compute scaling is a primary axis for improving LLM reasoning. Existing methods primarily scale depth by extending a single reasoning trace. Scaling breadth by sampling multiple candidates in parallel is straightforward, but introduces a selection bottleneck: choosing the best candidate without a ground-truth verifier, since pointwise LLM judging is noisy and biased. To address this, we introduce OpenDeepThink, a population-based test-time compute framework that selects via pairwise Bradley-Terry comparison. Each generation, the LLM judges random pairs of candidates and aggregates votes via Bradley-Terry into a global ranking; top-ranked candidates are preserved and the top three quarters are mutated using the natural-language critiques produced during comparison; the bottom quarter is discarded. OpenDeepThink raises Gemini 3.1 Pro's effective Codeforces Elo by +405 points in eight sequential LLM-call rounds (~27 minutes wall-clock). The pipeline transfers across weaker and stronger models without retuning, and on the multi-domain HLE benchmark, gains appear concentrated in objectively verifiable domains and reverse in subjective ones. We release CF-73, a curated set of 73 expert-rated Codeforces problems with International Grandmaster annotation and 99% local-evaluation agreement against the official verdict.

</details>

### [254] [Function-Correction with Optimal Data Protection for the General Hamming Code Membership](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14023)
*Adityawardhan Yadava,Anjana A. Mahesh,Swaraj Sharma Durgi*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究 Hamming 码成员函数的单错纠函数纠错码，证明有效奇偶分配条件与距离 3 码字图的连通二部结构，构造出最优最小距离为 2 的 SEFCC；进一步把减少距离 2 码字对的问题化为 max-cut 和谱图问题，并证明偶数 n 时 bent 函数可实现最优设计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对一般 n≥2 的 Hamming code membership function（HCMF），研究如何构造单错纠函数纠错码（SEFCC），并在保证函数纠错能力的同时优化码字间距离结构。

Method: 首先建立有效奇偶校验分配的充要条件，证明距离为 3 的码字图对所有 n≥2 诱导连通二部结构；据此构造最小距离达到最大可能值 2 的系统性 SEFCC。随后将距离为 2 的码字对最小化问题转化为两个部集上距离为 4 图的 max-cut 问题，并用最小特征值对应特征向量给出最优奇偶分配。进一步通过相关函数 Walsh 系数矩优化来求解特征向量，并在偶数 n 情形下借助 bent 函数达到紧下界。

Result: 论文得到了一种系统性 SEFCC 构造，其最小距离达到理论上最大可能值 2；同时证明距离 2 码字对的优化可由距离 4 图的 max-cut 及最小特征值特征向量刻画。对于偶数 n，最优结构可由 bent Boolean functions 实现。

Conclusion: 该工作完整刻画了 HCMF 的 SEFCC 奇偶分配条件，并揭示了最优 SEFCC 设计与谱图理论、max-cut 以及 bent Boolean 函数之间的精确联系，特别是在偶数 n 时给出了达到最优的构造依据。

Abstract: This paper investigates single-error-correcting function-correcting codes~(SEFCCs) for the $[2^n-1,\,2^n-1-n,\,3]$-Hamming code membership function~(HCMF) for general $n\geq 2$. Necessary and sufficient conditions for valid parity assignments are established, and the distance-$3$ codeword graph is shown to induce a connected bipartite structure for all $n\geq 2$, which is exploited to develop a systematic SEFCC construction achieving the largest possible minimum distance of~$2$. A novel framework is then developed that reduces the minimization of distance-$2$ codeword pairs to a max-cut problem on the distance-$4$ graphs of the two partite sets. Eigenvectors corresponding to the minimum eigenvalue of these graphs are shown to directly yield optimal parity assignments. We reduce the problem of finding these eigenvectors to an optimization problem involving moments of the Walsh coefficients of a related function, which we solve for even~$n$ by deriving a tight lower bound shown to be attained by bent functions, establishing a precise connection between optimal SEFCC design and bent Boolean functions.

</details>


### [255] [Multiple-Bases Belief Propagation List Decoding for Quantum LDPC Codes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14170)
*Sheida Rabeti,Hessam Mahdavifar*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文提出MBBP-LD量子LDPC译码器：通过构造多个无环子树导出的冗余校验表示并行运行BP，在保持BP线性复杂度和低延迟的同时提升译码性能；实验显示其在多种QLDPC码上优于BP-OSD和BPGD，且迭代次数更少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子低密度奇偶校验（QLDPC）码需要高效且高性能的译码器。标准BP译码复杂度低但受短环和退化性影响，性能有限；BP-OSD等方法虽能提升性能，却引入超线性后处理和较高延迟。因此论文希望在保持BP线性复杂度与并行效率的同时，提高QLDPC译码性能。

Method: 提出Multiple-Bases Belief-Propagation List Decoder（MBBP-LD）。方法通过对Tanner图进行无环子树分解，构造多个结构化的冗余校验矩阵表示，并在这些不同表示上并行运行BP译码，从而形成结构化译码多样性。该方法将经典MBBP框架扩展到量子码场景，并避免依赖超线性后处理。

Result: 仿真表明，MBBP-LD在多个QLDPC码上优于或不弱于现有BP类译码器，包括BP-OSD和BPGD，同时所需总BP迭代次数更少。在双变量bicycle码[[144,12,12]]与[[288,12,18]]上，低到中等错误率区间内，相比BPGD错误率最多降低20%，相比BP-OSD最多降低30%。在更大的B1码[[882,24,18≤d≤24]]上，其性能与BPGD相当或更优，并在并行实现下保持接近BP的译码延迟。

Conclusion: MBBP-LD通过多冗余校验表示带来的结构化多样性，有效缓解了标准BP在QLDPC码上的性能瓶颈，在不引入高复杂度后处理的情况下提升译码性能，适合低延迟并行实现，是一种兼具效率与性能的量子LDPC译码方案。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a belief-propagation (BP)-based decoder, termed the Multiple-Bases Belief-Propagation List Decoder (MBBP-LD), for quantum low-density parity-check (QLDPC) codes. The key idea is to generate \emph{structured decoding diversity} by constructing multiple redundant parity-check representations via cycle-free subtree decompositions of the Tanner graph, and running BP decoding in parallel across these representations. This extends the classical Multiple-Bases Belief-Propagation (MBBP) framework to the quantum setting while preserving the linear-time complexity and efficiency of standard BP decoding, and avoids the need for super-linear post-processing.
  Simulation results demonstrate that MBBP-LD improves upon existing BP-based decoders, including BP with ordered statistics decoding (BP-OSD) and belief propagation with guided decimation (BPGD) across several QLDPC codes, while requiring substantially fewer total BP iterations. For bivariate bicycle codes $[[144,12,12]]$ and $[[288,12,18]]$, MBBP-LD achieves up to $20\%$ reduction in error rate compared to BPGD and up to $30\%$ compared to BP-OSD in the low- and moderate-error regimes. For the larger B1 code $[[882, 24, 18 \leq d \leq 24]]$, MBBP-LD attains comparable or improved performance relative to BPGD while maintaining BP-like decoding latency under parallel implementation.

</details>


### [256] [Univariate Bicycle Quantum LDPC Codes: Explicit Logical Structure and Distance Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14173)
*Sheida Rabeti,Hessam Mahdavifar*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 论文提出UB量子LDPC码，用Frobenius关系把GB码的双多项式搜索简化为单多项式搜索，并给出逻辑算符的完整代数参数化和最小距离上界；仿真表明其在中小规模下性能接近或可比现有GB/BB码。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义自行车（GB）量子LDPC码通常需要在两个多项式上搜索，设计空间较大。论文希望通过引入更受约束但仍保持稀疏性的结构化子类，降低构造与分析复杂度，同时保持较好的码性能。

Method: 提出单变量自行车（UB）码：利用Frobenius关系将GB码的双多项式构造约化为单多项式构造；进一步通过代数方法构造逻辑商空间的基，完整参数化逻辑算符；并将结构化逻辑代表与相关循环矩阵的环密度性质联系起来，以推导最小距离上界。

Result: 在几百到约1000量级的短至中等长度码上，仿真显示UB码即使受到额外代数约束，仍相对于已有GB码和双变量自行车（BB）码具有竞争力。

Conclusion: UB码在显著缩小搜索空间、保持LDPC稀疏结构的同时，仍能实现有竞争力的量子纠错性能；其明确的逻辑空间刻画也为距离分析和码设计提供了便利。

Abstract: We introduce univariate bicycle (UB) codes, a structured subclass of generalized bicycle (GB) quantum low-density parity-check (LDPC) codes obtained via a Frobenius relation. This construction reduces the code design space from a two-polynomial search in GB codes to a single-polynomial search, while preserving sparsity. We provide an explicit algebraic characterization of the logical coset spaces by constructing a basis for the logical quotient space, yielding a complete parametrization of logical operators. Leveraging this structure, we derive upper bounds on the minimum distance by relating structured logical representatives to cycle-density properties of associated circulant matrices. Finally, simulation results for short- to medium-length UB codes (block lengths ranging from a few hundred to approximately $10^3$) demonstrate competitive performance relative to existing GB and bivariate bicycle (BB) codes despite the additional algebraic restriction.

</details>


### [257] [Capacity Characterization and Formation Optimization for Multi-User MIMO Communications with UAV Swarm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14298)
*Yong Zeng*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究 UAV 集群作为可控用户时 MU-MIMO 的最大和容量与最优编队，推导闭式容量表达式，并提出考虑避碰和凝聚约束的编队优化算法。核心发现是：UAV 协同移动可显著增强容量；ULA 下可同时获得 M 阶空间复用和 M 阶波束成形增益，UPA 下约 πM/4 个用户可同时享受满波束成形增益。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统以人为中心的 MU-MIMO 通信中用户位置随机且不可控，而面向地面/空中机器人尤其是 UAV 集群的新型应用中，用户位置可协同控制，因此需要回答可控用户位置下最大和容量及最优位置/编队这一基础问题。

Method: 论文先推导 MU-MIMO UAV 集群通信和容量的闭式表达式，分析 ULA/UPA 基站阵列下可移动性带来的空间复用与波束成形增益；随后构建 UAV 集群编队优化框架，分别针对 SIC 和 TIN 的和容量/和速率最大化，并纳入避碰与集群凝聚约束；利用阵列响应向量关于 UAV 方向的流形结构设计高效非凸优化算法。

Result: 结果表明，UAV 集群的协同机动自由度相较传统 MU-MIMO 可显著提升容量。对于配备 M 元 ULA 的基站，可同时实现完整空间复用增益 M 与完整波束成形增益 M；对于 UPA，渐近情况下约 πM/4 个用户可同时获得完整波束成形增益 M。仿真显示所提编队优化算法达到近最优性能。

Conclusion: 可控 UAV 用户位置为 MU-MIMO 系统提供了额外自由度，使系统能够通过优化集群编队显著提升容量，并在特定阵列结构下同时或大规模获得空间复用与波束成形收益；所提基于流形结构的算法能有效求解实际约束下的非凸编队优化问题。

Abstract: For a multi-user multiple-input multiple-output (MU-MIMO) wireless communication system, imagining that the locations of the users are now fully controllable, what is the maximum sum-capacity, and what are the corresponding optimal user locations? While these questions are irrelevant in conventional human-centric communications with random user mobility, they become critically important for emerging applications involving ground or aerial robots. This paper addresses these fundamental questions in the context of MU-MIMO communications with an unmanned aerial vehicle (UAV) swarm acting as the users. To this end, we first derive closed-form expressions for the sum-capacity of MU-MIMO UAV swarm communications. Our results reveal that, compared to conventional MU-MIMO systems, the additional degrees of freedom provided by the coordinated mobility of the UAV swarm yields substantial capacity enhancement. Specifically, when the base station (BS) is equipped with an $M$-element uniform linear array (ULA), the full spatial multiplexing gain and beamforming gain, both equal to $M$, can be achieved simultaneously. For a BS with a uniform planar array (UPA), we show that asymptotically $\frac{πM}{4}$ users can simultaneously enjoy the full beamforming gain $M$. Furthermore, we propose a novel framework to optimize UAV swarm formation for maximizing the sum-capacity achieved by successive interference cancellation (SIC) and maximizing the sum-rate via treating interference as noise (TIN), taking into account practical considerations such as collision avoidance and swarm cohesion constraints. By exploiting the manifold structure of the array response vectors with respect to UAV directions, we develop an efficient algorithm to solve the resulting non-convex formation optimization problems. Extensive simulation results demonstrate that the proposed algorithms achieve near-optimal performance.

</details>


### [258] [Secure Joint Source-Channel Coding of Multimodal Semantic Sources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14334)
*Denis Kozlov,Mahtab Mirmohseni,Rahim Tafazolli*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文研究多模态语义源经噪声窃听信道安全传输的问题，将率-失真-感知框架扩展到多模态场景，并给出传输率、失真/感知质量和保密性的可达与反 converse 界，表明保密极限由压缩、密钥率和信道统计共同决定。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 多模态语义源（如图像、音频、传感器数据）在噪声窃听信道上传输时，需要同时满足可靠重构、语义/感知质量与信息安全需求；现有单模态或传统安全源信道编码理论不足以刻画该场景的基本极限。

Method: 论文将率-失真-感知问题扩展到多模态源，建立包含 m 个模态、任意非空模态子集观测、离散无记忆窃听信道传输、合法接收端重构所有模态的模型；在逐模态失真与感知约束、逐子集含糊度约束下，推导传输率、保真度和保密性的 converse 与 achievability bounds。

Result: 论文给出了安全多模态联合源信道编码的基本性能界限，并指出保密性的基本极限由三个在操作意义上不同的部分共同决定：压缩水平、密钥率以及窃听信道统计特性。

Conclusion: 该工作为多模态语义源在噪声窃听信道中的安全传输提供了信息论刻画，揭示了压缩、密钥资源和信道安全性之间的权衡关系。

Abstract: We study the problem of secure joint source-channel coding for multimodal semantic sources transmitted over noisy wiretap channels. The source model consists of $m$ modalities (e.g., image, audio, and sensor data), all represented as random variables. The encoder observes independent and identically distributed samples of an arbitrary non-empty subset of modalities. The samples are encoded and transmitted over a discrete memoryless wiretap channel. The legitimate receiver reconstructs all modalities. We extend the rate-distortion-perception problem formulation to multimodal sources. We establish converse and achievability bounds on the fundamental limits of transmission rate, fidelity, and secrecy, under per-modality distortion and perception constraints, and per-subset equivocation constraints. We show that the fundamental limit for secrecy consists of three operationally distinct components: the level of compression, the secret key rate, and the statistics of the wiretap channel.

</details>


### [259] [CP-OFDM Achieves Lower Ranging CRB Than Frequency-Spread Waveforms in the Large-Sample Regime](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14451)
*Fan Liu,Yifeng Xiong,Ya-Feng Liu,Jie Yang,Christos Masouros,Shi Jin*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文从FIM结构分解出发证明，在随机通信符号复用感知时，CP-OFDM通常能比SC、OTFS、AFDM等波形实现更低的测距/幅度估计CRB，尤其在PSK下达到理论下界，在大符号数QAM/次高斯场景下具有渐近最优优势。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: ISAC中通信符号的随机性一方面允许感知复用通信资源，另一方面会引入波形相关的随机波动并影响测距精度。论文旨在回答：当感知复用随机数据信号时，调制波形如何影响测距CRB。

Method: 论文推导联合时延-幅度估计的Fisher信息矩阵结构分解，将目标几何的确定性Jacobian与由数据符号诱导的随机频域信号功率分离；建立Jensen型通用CRB下界；针对QAM和更一般的次高斯星座，采用逆FIM的渐近扰动分析；并在酉群上分析随机CRB优化问题的局部几何、驻点与Riemannian Hessian。

Result: CP-OFDM在PSK星座下精确达到Jensen型通用下界；在QAM及次高斯星座下，当发送符号数N足够大且随机FIM可逆时，CP-OFDM相较任何频域扩展正交波形获得更低的测距CRB。该优势还扩展到幅度估计及联合时延-幅度估计。数值实验表明OFDM优于SC、OTFS和AFDM等代表性波形。

Conclusion: CP-OFDM在随机数据符号复用感知的ISAC场景中具有理论上的CRB优势：PSK下全局达到通用下界，QAM/次高斯情形下表现出渐近优势，并且在酉群优化意义下具有渐近局部最优性。

Abstract: The inherent randomness of communication symbols creates a fundamental tension in Integrated Sensing and Communications (ISAC). On the one hand, they enable data transmission while allowing sensing to fully reuse communication resources. On the other hand, their randomness induces waveform-dependent fluctuations that directly affect sensing accuracy. This paper investigates a foundational question arising from this tradeoff: \textit{How does the modulation waveform affect the ranging Cramér--Rao Bound (CRB) when sensing reuses random data symbols?} We address this question by revealing a structural factorization of the Fisher information matrix (FIM) for joint delay-amplitude estimation, which separates the deterministic Jacobian of the target geometry from the random frequency-domain signal power induced by the data symbols. This structure yields a Jensen-type universal lower bound on the CRB, which is exactly attained by CP-OFDM under PSK constellations. For QAM and broader sub-Gaussian constellations, we develop an asymptotic perturbation analysis of the inverse FIM and prove that, when the number of transmitted symbols $N$ grows large, CP-OFDM achieves a lower ranging CRB than any frequency-spread orthogonal waveform over the almost-sure event where the random FIM is invertible. This superiority is further extended to amplitude estimation and full joint delay-amplitude estimation. We also characterize the local geometry of the stochastic CRB minimization problem over the unitary group. The analysis reveals that CP-OFDM is a stationary point for finite $N$, and its Riemannian Hessian is positive semidefinite for sufficiently large $N$, establishing its asymptotic local optimality. Numerical results confirm that OFDM outperforms representative waveforms including SC, OTFS, and AFDM.

</details>


### [260] [Quaternary codes with new parameters from two-generator simplicial complexes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14603)
*Ankit Yadav,Nilay Kumar Mondal,Ritumoni Sarma*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文用二生成元单纯复形构造无限族 Z4 线性码，确定 Lee 重量分布，发现多组新的/改进的最佳已知四元码，并刻画 Gray 像线性的条件，进一步得到 Griesmer 码和极小二元线性码族。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 构造并研究新的四元（Z4 上）线性码族，以获得更优参数的四元码，并分析其 Gray 像在线性性、Griesmer 码与极小二元线性码方面的性质。

Method: 利用由二生成元单纯复形导出的定义集 D 构造无限族 quaternary C_D-codes，并推导其 Lee 重量分布；进一步分析 Gray 映射后的线性条件。

Result: 得到至少 32 个新的或改进的四元线性码，包括来自 Plotkin 最优族的码；还报告了 6 个具有最佳已知参数的投影四元线性码，并给出 Gray 像线性的充要条件，从而导出无限族 Griesmer 码和若干无限族极小二元线性码。

Conclusion: 该工作通过单纯复形方法系统构造了性能优良的四元线性码族，不仅扩展了最佳已知四元码数据库，还建立了其 Gray 像与经典二元线性码最优性、极小性之间的联系。

Abstract: In this article, we construct infinite families of quaternary (that is, over the ring $\mathbb{Z}_4$) $\mathcal{C}_{D}$-codes, where the defining set $D$ is derived utilizing a two-generator simplicial complex, and determine their Lee weight distributions. As a result, we find at least 32 new or improved quaternary linear codes as per the database \cite{aydin2022updated} of best-known quaternary codes, including codes from a Plotkin-optimal family. We also report 6 projective quaternary linear codes with best-known parameters that might outperform the currently reported best-known codes due to their projectivity. Further, we establish necessary and sufficient conditions for their Gray image to be linear, which in turn gives an infinite family of Griesmer codes and several infinite families of minimal binary linear codes.

</details>


### [261] [LLM-Enabled Automated Algorithm Design for Multiuser Fluid Antenna Communications](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14661)
*Gan Zheng,Fei Liu,Qingfu Zhang*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文用大语言模型自动设计流体天线端口选择优化算法，通过改进遗传算法和设计 AutoPort，在最大化最小 SINR 的公平性问题上实现接近最优且优于传统 GA 与深度学习的性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 流体天线可通过动态调整辐射端口/位置为无线通信提供新的自由度，但端口选择属于大规模组合优化问题，难以用传统人工启发式方法高效求解；现有方法依赖人工调参且性能有限。

Method: 论文提出利用大语言模型自动设计流体天线系统优化算法，面向下行链路最大化用户间最小 SINR 的公平性目标，联合优化端口选择与波束成形。具体研究两种 LLM 驱动策略：一是自动优化遗传算法中的交叉与变异操作；二是由 LLM 从零设计新的启发式算法 AutoPort。

Result: 仿真结果表明，LLM 设计的方法能够取得接近最优的性能，并显著优于传统遗传算法和深度学习方法。

Conclusion: LLM 可作为自动化算法设计工具，有效替代人工超启发式调参，为流体天线端口选择等复杂无线通信组合优化问题提供高性能、低人工成本的求解范式。

Abstract: Fluid antenna is a new reconfigurable antenna technology that can dynamically adjust the positions or ports of radiating elements and therefore provides a new degree of freedom for wireless communications. However, the associated port selection is a challenging large-scale combinatorial optimization problem and difficult to solve. Existing manually designed heuristic algorithms are not only labor-intensive, but cannot achieve satisfactory performance. In this paper, we propose a novel paradigm that leverages large language models (LLMs) for automated design of optimization algorithms for fluid antenna systems without manual hyperheuristic tuning. Specifically, we study the problem of maximizing the minimum signal-to-interference-plus-noise ratio (SINR) in the downlink to ensure fairness among users by optimizing port selection and beamforming. We investigate two LLM-enabled algorithm optimization strategies. The first is to optimize the crossover and mutation operations to enhance the performance of the well-known genetic algorithm and the second is to design AutoPort, a new heuristic from scratch by LLM, to solve the optimization problem. Simulation results verify that the proposed method can achieve near-optimal performance and significant improvement over the conventional genetic algorithm and the deep learning approach.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于特殊 Weil 和构造一类线性认证码，并利用 Weil 和相关性质计算替换攻击与冒充攻击的最大成功概率。

### [263] [Construction of Minimal Ternary Linear Codes with Dimension $n+2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2605.14848)
*Haibo Liu,Xin Guo,Qunying Liao*

Main category: cs.IT

TL;DR: 本文构造了一类新的三元极小线性码：它们维数为 m+2，违反 Ashikhmin-Barg 条件，但仍可通过论文给出的充要条件证明其极小性，并利用指数和确定完整重量枚举子。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 极小线性码因其在秘密共享、安全两方计算等密码学场景中的应用而受到关注。构造违反 Ashikhmin-Barg 条件但仍保持极小性的线性码，并确定其重量分布，是编码理论中的重要问题。

Method: 论文提出一种维数为 m+2 的三元线性码通用构造，推导该码为极小码的充要条件；随后结合该条件与指数和技术，构造新的三元极小线性码类，并分析其完全重量枚举子。

Result: 得到了一类违反 Ashikhmin-Barg 条件的新三元极小线性码，并确定了这些码的完全重量枚举子，从而给出更精细的重量分布信息。

Conclusion: 该研究扩展了已知极小三元线性码的构造范围，证明即使不满足 Ashikhmin-Barg 条件，也可以通过特定代数构造获得极小线性码，并精确刻画其重量结构。

Abstract: Recently, minimal linear codes have been extensively studied due to their applications in secret sharing schemes, secure two-party computations, and so on. Constructing minimal linear codes violating the Ashikhmin-Barg condition and then determining their weight distributions have been interesting in coding theory and cryptography. In this paper, a generic construction for ternary linear codes with dimension $m+2$ is presented, where $m$ is an integer, and a necessary and sufficient condition for this ternary linear code to be minimal is derived. Based on this condition and exponential sums, a new class of minimal ternary linear codes violating the Ashikhmin-Barg condition are obtained, and then their complete weight enumerators are determined.

</details>
